another thing i worry about in the global commons is the threat posed by trafficking , by the movement of narcotics , opium , here coming out of afghanistan through europe over to the united states .	在全球公有物讓我擔心的另一件事是人口販賣的威脅 , 造成麻醉劑、鴉片等毒品的移動 , 從阿富汗穿過歐洲到美國 。
we worry about cocaine coming from the andean ridge north .	我們擔心從andeanridge北部運過來的可卡因
we worry about the movement of illegal weapons and trafficking . above all , perhaps , we worry about human trafficking , and the awful cost of it .	我們擔心非法武器的運行和販賣 。 最重要的是 , 我們擔心人口販賣 , 以及它的糟糕代價 。
trafficking moves largely at sea but in other parts of the global commons .	大部分的人口販賣活動是在海上 , 但在全球公有物的其他地方 。
this is a photograph , and i wish i could tell you that this is a very hightech piece of us navy gear that we're using to stop the trafficking .	這是一張照片 , 我希望我能告訴你 , 這是美國海軍陸戰火裝的高科技片段 , 我們用它來阻止人口販運 。
the bad news is , this is a semisubmersible run by drug cartels .	壞消息是 , 這是一個販毒集團的半潛水器
it was built in the jungles of south america .	在南美洲的叢林中被建造
we caught it with that lowtech raft — — and it was carrying six tons of cocaine .	我們用那個低科技竹子逮到它 , 它帶著六噸的可卡因 。
crew of four . sophisticated communications sweep .	四名船員 , 精良的通訊總共橫掃了
this kind of trafficking , in narcotics , in humans , in weapons , god forbid , in weapons of mass destruction , is part of the threat to the global commons .	這種販賣 , 在毒品上 , 在人身上 , 在武器上 , 上帝禁止 , 在大規模毀滅性武器中 , 是威脅全球公有物的一部分 。
and let's pull it together in afghanistan today .	讓我們一起在今天的阿富汗
this is a field of poppies in afghanistan .	這是在阿富汗的一片乾草田 ,
eighty to 90 percent of the world's poppy , opium and heroin , comes out of afghanistan .	全世界80%到90%的貘 , 鴉片和海洛因是從阿富汗出來的
we also see there , of course , terrorism .	當然 , 我們也會看到恐怖主義 。
this is where al qaeda is staged from .	這是基地組織的出發點
we also see a very strong insurgency embedded there .	我們也看到了一場非常強烈的暴動就嵌在了那裡 。
so this terrorism concern is also part of the global commons , and what we must address .	所以 , 這種恐怖主義也是全球公有物的一部分 , 我們必須要處理的 。
so here we are , 21st century .	所以我們現在 , 21世紀
we know our 20thcentury tools are not going to work .	我們知道我們的20世紀工具是行不通的 。
what should we do ?	我們應該怎麼做 ?
i would argue that we will not deliver security solely from the barrel of a gun .	我認為我們不能僅僅依靠槍支來遞送安全 。
we will not deliver security solely from the barrel of a gun .	我們不能僅僅依靠槍支來遞送安全 。
we will need the application of military force .	我們需要軍事力量的應用
when we do it , we must do it well , and competently .	當我們著手進行時 , 我們必須表現得很好 , 而且要有能力 。
but my thesis is , opensource security is about international , interagency , privatepublic connection pulled together by this idea of strategic communication on the internet .	但我的論點是 , 開放式安全是關乎國際的 , 跨部門的 , 私人的和公共的聯系 , 由互聯網上策略性溝通的想法聚集在一起 。
let me give you a couple of examples of how this works in a positive way .	讓我舉幾個例子來說明這如何用正面的方式來進行
this is afghanistan . these are afghan soldiers .	這是阿富汗 。 這些是阿富汗士兵 。
they are all holding books .	他們都拿著書 。
you should say , " that's odd . i thought i read that this demographic , young men and women in their 20s and 30s , is largely illiterate in afghanistan . "	你應該說: 「 真奇怪 , 我以為我讀了這個人口 , 二十幾歲和三十幾歲的年輕人 , 在阿富汗也是不識字的 。 」
you would be correct .	你會是正確的 。
eightyfive percent cannot read when they enter the security forces of afghanistan .	當他們進入阿富汗的安全部隊時 , 85%是無法閱讀的 。
why ? because the taliban withheld education during the period of time in which these men and women would have learned to read .	為什麼 ? 因為塔利班的教育 , 在這段時間裡 , 男性和女性都能學會閱讀 。
so the question is , so , why are they all standing there holding books ?	所以問題是 , 為什麼他們都站在那裏拿著書 ?
the answer is , we are teaching them to read in literacy courses by nato in partnership with private sector entities , in partnership with development agencies .	答案是 , 我們在教導他們讀書 , 在北約組織課程 , 和私營機構合作 , 和發展機構合作 。
we've taught well over 200 , 000 afghan security forces to read and write at a basic level .	我們已經教了超過二十萬名阿富汗安全部隊士兵 , 基本上他們會讀和寫 。
when you can read and write in afghanistan , you will typically put a pen in your pocket .	當你可以在阿富汗閱讀和寫作時 , 你通常會在你的口袋裡放一支筆 。
at the ceremonies , when these young men and women graduate , they take that pen with great pride , and put it in their pocket .	在畢業典禮上 , 當這些年輕男女畢業時 , 他們很驕傲地拿下那筆 , 放在他們的口袋裡 。
this is bringing together international — there are 50 nations involved in this mission — interagency — these development agencies — and privatepublic , to take on this kind of security .	這也讓各國團結起來 , 共有50個國家參與這個使命 , 各部門 , 各部門 , 私人和公共和公共 , 致力於這種安全 。
now , we are also teaching them combat skills , of course , but i would argue , opensource security means connecting in ways that create longer lasting security effect .	當然 , 我們也在教導他們對抗技能 , 但我認為 , 開放式安全意味著用能夠創造更持久的安全的方式來聯繫 。
this is a us navy warship .	這是美國海軍戰艦 。
it's called the comfort .	所謂的舒適
there's a sister ship called the mercy .	有一艘叫作慈悲的姊妹船
they are hospital ships .	他們是醫院 。
this one , the comfort , operates throughout the caribbean and the coast of south america conducting patient treatments .	這個 , 安慰號在加勒比海和南美洲的海岸進行病人的治療 。
on a typical cruise , they'll do 400 , 000 patient treatments .	在典型的巡迴演出中 , 他們會進行40萬次病人治療 。
it is crewed not strictly by military but by a combination of humanitarian organizations: operation hope , project smile .	船員不是被軍隊嚴格對待 , 而是被人道主義組織合併:希望、專案微笑 。
other organizations send volunteers .	其他組織送來志願者
interagency physicians come out .	國際間的醫生走出來 ,
they're all part of this .	他們都是這件作品的一部分 。
to give you one example of the impact this can have , this little boy , eight years old , walked with his mother two days to come to the eye clinic put on by the comfort .	舉個例子讓你們看看這個小男孩 , 八歲 , 跟著他媽媽走了兩天 , 來到安慰號上的眼科診所 。
when he was fitted , over his extremely myopic eyes , he suddenly looked up and said , " mama , veo el mundo . "	當他被治好的時候 , 在他那極為神秘的雙眼底下 , 他突然抬頭說: 「 mama , veoelmundo 。 」
" mom , i see the world . "	" 媽 , 我看到世界了 。 "
multiply this by 400 , 000 patient treatments , this privatepublic collaboration with security forces , and you begin to see the power of creating security in a very different way .	把這個乘以400 , 000的病患治療 , 這個私人和公共的合作 , 加上安全力量 , 你就會開始看到用截然不同的方式創造安全的力量 。
here you see baseball players .	這裡你看到棒球選手
can you pick out the two us army soldiers in this photograph ?	你能挑出這張照片中的兩名美國軍人嗎 ?
they are the two young men on either side of these young boys . this is part of a series of baseball clinics , where we have explored collaboration between major league baseball , the department of state , who sets up the diplomatic piece of this , military baseball players , who are real soldiers with real skills but participate in this mission , and they put on clinics throughout latin america and the caribbean , in honduras , in nicaragua , in all of the central american and caribbean nations where baseball is so popular , and it creates security .	他們是兩位年輕男孩兩方面的年輕人 。 這是棒球診所的一部分 。 在那裡 , 我們探討了聯盟棒球聯賽 , 國務院 , 設立了美軍棒球隊 , 他們是真正有技能的軍人 , 參與了這場使命 , 他們考慮了拉丁美洲和加勒比海 , 橫跨跨跨整個美洲和加勒比海 , 開到了所有美洲 , 開到了賽道上 。
it shows role models to young men and women about fitness and about life that i would argue help create security for us .	它向年輕男女展示了關于健身和人生的榜樣 , 我主張協助為我們創造安全 。
another aspect of this partnership is in disaster relief .	這個合作的另一方面是救災行動
this is a us air force helicopter participating after the tsunami in 2004 which killed 250 , 000 people .	這是美國空軍的直升機2004年參與海嘯殺死25萬人
in each of these major disasters — the tsunami in 2004 , 250 , 000 dead , the kashmiri earthquake in pakistan , 2005 , 85 , 000 dead , the haitian earthquake , about 300 , 000 dead , more recently the awful earthquaketsunami combination which struck japan and its nuclear industry — in all of these instances , we see partnerships between international actors , interagency , privatepublic working with security forces to respond to this kind of natural disaster .	在所有這些重大災難中2004年海嘯 , 25萬人死亡 , 2005年巴基斯坦的喀什米里地震 , 8萬5千人死亡 , 海地地震 , 大約30萬人死亡 , 更近期就是那些糟糕的地震海嘯雙重打擊日本和其核能產業 。 在所有這些例子中 , 我們看到了國際間 , 跨部門 , 公私結合的合作 , 使得人們能夠得到安全的保護 。
so these are examples of this idea of opensource security .	所以這些都是關於公開資源安全的例子
we tie it together , increasingly , by doing things like this .	我們將它綁在一起 , 漸漸地 , 通過這樣做
now , you're looking at this thinking , " ah , admiral , these must be sea lanes of communication , or these might be fiber optic cables . "	現在 , 你看到這個想法: 「 啊 , 馬達 , 這些一定是通信電纜線 , 或者這些可能是光纖電纜 。 」
no . this is a graphic of the world according to twitter .	不是的 。 這是twitter世界的圖像 。
purple are tweets . green are geolocation .	紫色是推特 , 綠色是地緣分配 。
white is the synthesis .	白色是綜合體 。
it's a perfect evocation of that great population survey , the six largest nations in the world in descending order: china , india , facebook , the united states , twitter and indonesia .	這是個完美的驅動了那次人口普查 , 六個世界最大的國家依次是:中國 , 印度 , 臉書 , 美國 , 推特和印尼 。
why do we want to get in these nets ?	我們為什麼要拿到這些蚊帳
why do we want to be involved ?	我們為什麼想參與 ?
we talked earlier about the arab spring , and the power of all this .	我們之前談到阿拉伯之春 , 以及這一切的力量 。
i'll give you another example , and it's how you move this message .	我再舉一個例子 , 它是你如何移動這個訊息 。
i gave a talk like this in london a while back about this point . i said , as i say to all of you , i'm on facebook . friend me .	前陣子我在倫敦做過這樣的演講 , 關於這點 。 我對你們說 , 我在facebook上 。 朋友 。
got a little laugh from the audience .	從觀眾中得到一陣笑聲 。
there was an article which was run by ap , on the wire .	有一篇文章是ap , 在電纜線上執行 。
got picked up in two places in the world: finland and indonesia .	被世界上兩個地方接起來:芬蘭和印尼 。
the headline was: nato admiral needs friends .	標題是:北約艦隊司令需要好友 。
and the story was a catalyst , and the next morning i had hundreds of facebook friend requests from indonesians and finns , mostly saying , " admiral , we heard you need a friend , and oh , by the way , what is nato ? "	故事是種催化劑 , 隔天早上 , 我收到上百個臉書朋友的請求 , 來自印尼和芬蘭 , 大部分都會說: 「 司機 , 我們聽說你需要一個朋友 , 哦 , 順帶一提 , nato是甚麼 ? 」
yeah , we laugh , but this is how we move the message , and moving that message is how we connect international , interagency , privatepublic , and these social nets to help create security .	是啊 , 我們笑了 , 但這就是我們如何移動訊息 , 而那訊息就是我們如何連結國際 , 跨部門 , 私人和公共 , 還有這些社交網 , 來協助創造安全 。
now , let me hit a somber note .	現在 , 讓我用一個嚴肅的語調
this is a photograph of a brave british soldier .	這是一張勇敢的英國士兵的照片 。
he's in the scots guards .	他在蘇格蘭護衛隊
he's standing the watch in helmand , in southern afghanistan .	他正站在hlmand的立場 , 在阿富汗南部 。
i put him here to remind us , i would not want anyone to leave the room thinking that we do not need capable , competent militaries who can create real military effect .	我把他放到這裡來提醒我們 , 我不會讓任何人離開房間 , 認為我們不需要 , 強壯的軍隊能夠創造真正的軍事效果 。
that is the core of who we are and what we do , and we do it to protect freedom , freedom of speech , all the things we treasure in our societies .	這是我們是誰的核心我們做的事是為了保護自由 , 言論自由我們在社會中珍視的所有事
but , you know , life is not an onandoff switch .	但 , 要知道 , 人生並非一時即興的開關 。
you don't have to have a military that is either in hard combat or is in the barracks .	你不需要有一支隊伍 , 不是在戰場上 , 就是在兵營裡 。
i would argue life is a rheostat .	我主張生活是一種表面
you have to dial it in , and as i think about how we create security in this 21st century , there will be times when we will apply hard power in true war and crisis , but there will be many instances , as we've talked about today , where our militaries can be part of creating 21stcentury security , international , interagency , privatepublic , connected with competent communication .	你必須將它付諸實行 , 正如我所想的 , 我們在21世紀如何創造安全 , 有時候我們會在真正的戰爭和危機中使用真正的權力 , 但會有很多案例 , 正如我們今天討論的 , 我們的軍隊能夠參與創造21世紀安全 , 國際 , 跨部門 , 公私結合 , 以能力交流 。
i would close by saying that we heard earlier today about wikipedia . i use wikipedia all the time to look up facts , and as all of you appreciate , wikipedia is not created by 12 brilliant people locked in a room writing articles .	在結束前 , 我想說 , 我們今天聽到的主題是關於維基百科 。 我經常使用維基百科查詢事實 , 正如你們所聽到的 , 維基百科並不是由12個聰明的人所創造的 , 鎖在一個房間寫文章
wikipedia , every day , is tens of thousands of people inputting information , and every day millions of people withdrawing that information .	維基百科 , 每天都有成千上萬的人在輸入資訊 , 每一天都有數百萬人在戒斷那些資訊 。
it's a perfect image for the fundamental point that no one of us is as smart as all of us thinking together .	這是完美的圖像 , 對於根本的重點 , 我們沒有人能像所有人一樣聰明 。
no one person , no one alliance , no one nation , no one of us is as smart as all of us thinking together .	沒有一個人 , 沒有一個聯盟 , 沒有一個國家 , 沒有一個人像我們所有人一樣聰明 。
the vision statement of wikipedia is very simple: a world in which every human being can freely share in the sum of all knowledge .	維基百科的宣言很簡單:一個人人都可以自由地分享所有知識的世界 。
my thesis for you is that by combining international , interagency , privatepublic , strategic communication , together , in this 21st century , we can create the sum of all security .	我的論點是 , 藉由結合國際 , 跨部門 , 私人和公共 , 戰略交流 , 一起在這個21世紀 , 我們能創造出所有安全的總和 。
thank you very much . thank you . thank you .	非常感謝 。 謝謝 。 謝謝 。
